# Sitemap Structural Duplicate Groups
This report groups Lowe's `/pl/` URLs by **base category id** (first numeric token in the last path segment).
Within a group, the URLs are usually refinements/filters for the same category, so we keep a single canonical URL (prefer unrefined `.../<id>` when present).
## Summary
- Total sitemap `/pl/` URLs (reconstructed): 497492
- Unique base category ids: 3597
- Structural minimal URL count: 3597
- Duplicate groups (base ids with >1 URL): 3596
- Skipped (couldn't parse a base id): 0
